therefore focuses\nonly on matters which are significant to the company.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" On 5 February 2015, the group was\nacquired by Stork Holdings Limited (Note 14).</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" Wharf.</span></ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" £10,856,305 (2013:\n£27,642,183). This includes the profits on disposal referred to above.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The balance sheet shows the company's financial position at the\nyear end and indicates that<a></a> net assets were £166,532,720\n(2013: £177,366,865). Details of amounts owed to group companies are shown in\nNote 9. </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The Canary Wharf Group (comprising Canary Wharf Group plc and its\nsubsidiaries) manages its<a></a> operations on a unified basis.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>For this reason, the company's directors\nbelieve that key<a></a> performance indicators specific to the\ncompany are not necessary or appropriate for an<a></a> understanding\nof the development, performance or position of its business.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The performance<a></a> of the\nCanary Wharf Group, which includes the company, is discussed in the Annual\nReport of<a></a> Canary Wharf Group plc, which does not form part of\nthis report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">As a member of the Canary Wharf Group the key risks facing the\ncompany include<a></a> the cyclical nature of the property market,\nfinancing risk and concentration risk.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Cyclical Nature of the Property Market</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The valuation of the Canary Wharf Group's assets is subject to\nmany external economic and<a></a> market factors. Following the\nturmoil in the financial markets and uncertainty in the Eurozone of recent\nyears, the London real estate market had to cope with a decline in demand and a\npotential oversupply of office space.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>The possible oversupply of available space in the market was, however,\nmitigated by the difficulty in securing finance for speculative development\nleading to reduced supply.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>The market\nwas assisted by the continuing presence of overseas investors attracted by the\nrelative transparency of the real estate market in London which is viewed as\nboth stable and secure. The market has also been underpinned by continuing\ndemand for sites capable of incorporating residential development. During 2014,\nthere was evidence of continuing investor demand for office space and\ncontinuing confidence in the office real estate market.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Changes in financial and property markets are kept under constant\nreview so that the company<a></a> can react appropriately and tailor\nits business accordingly.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;&#xD;&#xA;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Financing Risk</span></b><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The broader economic cycle inevitably leads to movements in\ninflation, interest rates and<a></a> bond yields. The company\nfinances its operations largely through surplus cash and intercompany finance.\nThe terms of the company's borrowings are summarised in Note 9.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Concentration Risk</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The majority of Canary Wharf Group's real estate assets, including\nthe assets of the<a></a> company, are currently located on or\nadjacent to the Canary Wharf Estate with a majority of<a></a>\ntenants linked to the financial services industry.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>Wherever possible steps are taken to<a></a> mitigate or avoid material consequences arising from this\nconcentration and to diversify<a></a> the tenant base.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">The principal risks facing the Canary Wharf Group are discussed in\nthe Annual Report of<a></a> Canary Wharf Group plc, which does not\nform part of this report.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection5\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">GOING CONCERN</span></b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">At the year end, the company is in a net asset position, but has\nnet current liabilities.<a></a> Included in this are group creditors\nof £255,546,483, which to the extent that the company cannot pay, will not be\ncalled in for at least a period of 12 months from the signing date of the\nfinancial statements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">In addition, as a member of the Canary Wharf Group, the company\nhas access to considerable resources.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">Having made the requisite enquiries and assessed the resources at\nthe disposal of the<a></a> company, the directors have a reasonable\nexpectation that the company will have adequate<a></a> resources to\ncontinue its operation for the foreseeable future. Accordingly they continue<a></a> to adopt the going concern basis in preparing the financial\nstatements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\">An audit involves obtaining evidence about the amounts and\ndisclosures in the financial<a></a> statements sufficient to give\nreasonable assurance that the financial statements are free<a></a>\nfrom material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or error.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>This includes an assessment<a></a>\nof: whether the accounting policies are appropriate to the company's\ncircumstances and have<a></a> been consistently applied and\nadequately disclosed; the reasonableness of significant<a></a>\naccounting estimates made by the directors; and the overall presentation of the\nfinancial<a></a> statements.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>In addition, we read all the financial and non-financial information in\nthe<a></a> Annual Report to identify material inconsistencies with\nthe audited financial statements and to identify any information that is\napparently materially incorrect based on, or<a></a> materially\ninconsistent with, the knowledge acquired by us in the course of performing the<a></a> audit. If we become aware of any apparent material\nmisstatements or inconsistencies we<a></a> consider the\nimplications for our report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" historical cost convention,<a></a>\n modified to include the revaluation of properties and in accordance with\n applicable United Kingdom accounting standards.</span></ix:nonNumeric></span> The financial\nstatements have been prepared on a going concern basis as described in the\nStrategic Report.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" of FRS 1\n (Revised) the company is exempt from<a></a> the requirements to\n prepare a cash flow statement, as it is a wholly-owned<a></a>\n subsidiary of Canary Wharf Group plc, which has prepared a consolidated cash\n flow<a></a> statement</span></ix:exclude><div style=\"display:none\">true</div></ix:nonNumeric></span>.</span></div><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><span><ix:nonNumeric name=\"ns4:TurnoverPolicy\" contextRef=\"CY_PERIOD\"><span style=\"background:white;mso-highlight:white\">Turnover represents rents\n receivable net of VAT and is recognised on an accruals basis in the period in\n which the rents become due.</span></ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Interest\nreceivable and interest payable</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Interest\nreceivable and payable are recognised on an accruals basis in the period in\nwhich they fall due.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Income\nfrom investments</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Investment\nincome comprises dividends paid by subsidiary undertakings during the\naccounting year.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Investment\nproperties</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Investment\nproperties are revalued annually and in accordance with SSAP 19 (Accounting for\nInvestment Properties) no provision is made for depreciation. This departure\nfrom the requirements of the statutory accounting rules, which requires all\nproperties to be depreciated is, in the opinion of the directors, necessary for\nthe accounts to show a true and fair view. Depreciation is only one of the\nfactors reflected in the annual valuation and the amount attributable to this\nfactor is not capable of being separately identified or quantified. Surpluses\nor deficits are transferred to the revaluation reserve, unless a deficit\nexceeds previous surpluses recognised on the same property, in which case the\nexcess is charged to the profit and loss account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Development\nproperties</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Properties\nunder development or held for development, comprising leasehold buildings and<a></a> freehold land, are held at cost, subject to provision for\ndiminution in value.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Investments</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Investments\nin subsidiaries are stated at cost less any provision for impairment.</span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection14\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade\nand other debtors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debtors\nare recognised initially at fair value.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> \n</span>A provision for impairment is established where there is objective evidence\nthat the company will not be able to collect all amounts due according to the\noriginal terms of the debtor concerned.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Trade\nand other creditors</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Trade\nand other creditors are stated at cost.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Debt</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Debt\ninstruments are stated initially at the amount of the net proceeds. The finance\ncosts of such debt instruments are allocated to periods over the term of the\ndebt at a constant rate on the carrying amount. The carrying amount is\nincreased by the finance cost in respect of the reporting period and reduced by\npayments made in respect of the debt of that period. Finance costs are charged\nto the profit and loss account.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span><b>Taxation</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Current\ntax is provided at amounts expected to be paid or recovered using the tax rates\nand laws that have been enacted or substantively enacted at the balance sheet\ndate. </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax assets and liabilities arise from timing differences between the recognition\nof gains and losses in the financial statements and their recognition in the\ncorporation tax return.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Under\nFRS 19 deferred tax is recognised in respect of all timing differences that\nhave originated but not reversed at the balance sheet date where transactions\nor events that result in an obligation to pay more tax in the future or a right\nto pay less tax in the future have occurred at the balance sheet date.<span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\">  </span>A net deferred tax asset is regarded as\nrecoverable and therefore recognised only when, on the basis of all available\nevidence, it can be regarded as more likely than not that there will be\nsuitable taxable profits from which the future reversal of the underlying\ntiming differences can be deducted.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is not recognised when fixed assets are revalued unless by the balance\nsheet date there is a binding agreement to sell the revalued assets and the\ngain or loss expected to arise on sale has been recognised in the financial\nstatements.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:0in;&#xD;&#xA;margin-left:23.2pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-23.2pt;&#xD;&#xA;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Deferred\ntax is measured on a discounted basis to reflect the time value of money over\nthe period between the balance sheet date and the dates on which it is\nestimated that the timing differences will reverse, or where the timing\ndifferences are not expected to reverse, a period not exceeding 50 years. <span style=\"mso-spacerun:yes\"> </span>Discount rates of 0.2% to 2.3% have been\nadopted reflecting the post-tax yield to maturity that can be obtained on\ngovernment bonds with similar maturity dates and currencies to those of the\ndeferred tax assets or liabilities.</span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:.5pt;mso-line-height-rule:exactly;mso-pagination:none;&#xD;&#xA;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"> </span></p></div><div></div><div><span style=\"font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;color:black;mso-ansi-language:EN-GB;&#xD;&#xA;mso-fareast-language:EN-GB;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA\"><br /></span></div><div></div><div class=\"WordSection15\"><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-size:9.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"> </span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;tab-stops:23.2pt;mso-layout-grid-align:&#xD;&#xA;none;text-autospace:none\"><a></a><b><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\">2.</span></b><a></a><span style=\"font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;&#xD;&#xA;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">     </span><b>OPERATING LOSS</b></span></p><p class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:&#xD;&#xA;justify;line-height:normal;mso-pagination:none;mso-layout-grid-align:none;&#xD;&#xA;text-autospace:none\"><span style=\"font-family:&#xD;&#xA;&quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;;color:black\"><span style=\"mso-tab-count:1\">        </span>Operating\nloss is stated after charging:</span></p><table
